ABANTU baka King William abaseThekwini inkosi yabaphatha ngaso isandla sikaShaka. Babengabantu "bomfowabo" ebukhosini ngakllO kumelwe ukuba bavikelwe yiyo. Ababili balaba esas;bajwayele base bafa sekusele bathathu kuphela baIabo ababeke basivakashele noShaka eminyakeni eyayedlule. Omkhulu kubo kwabe kunguFarewell owayeyindoda eqotho engahlehli, osefile kodwa manic, kanye noKing owayenomusa kakhuIu yena wafa masinyane nje emva kokubuya kwabo eKapa namanxusa. 

  UFebane wafa kanje. Kwathi ukuba kufe uShaka abantu ababekhonze kuye base bephathwa uDingane ngaphandle kwabakwaQwabe abamisa amakhanda uQwabe noZulu kwabe kungabafowabo ngakho abakwaQwabe nabakwaZu!u babehlobene. Kodwa abakwaQwabe babcyisizwe esikhudlwana kunesakwaZulu futhi ezinsukwini ezingaphambili kukaShaka babengesinye sezizwe ezinamandla kakhulu. UShaka wasemnqoba uPhakathwayo wamenza yena nabantu bakhe bakhonze kuye kodwa kuthe ekufeni kukaShaka uNqwetho owalandela uPhakathwayo wamdeIela uDingane wala ukuba akhonze kuye. Ezinye izintombi ngithi mhlawumbe zazilishumi zasuke zenqaba ukwendela ebuthweni ezazijutshelwe lona inkosi. Lezizintombi zephula umthetho wesizwe zibhekile ngamehlo azo, Ukuba zaqoma ukungathathi muntu wesilisa zazihlalela nje kwakungeke kube lutho kodwa zasuke zenza isiphosiso ngokuyozifunela abathandwa yizo. Inhlonipho yinto njena okumele ibekhona, Ngomthetho wezwe bahlawulwa ngenhlawulo eyayibafanele inhlawulo ababeyazi ukuthi iyobafikela, Thina sasingenamatilongo. Lena kwabe kungeyona (ngokueabanga kwenkosi nebandla layo) indaba eyayifuna ingenwe ngabantu bangaphandle kodwa uHulumeni wamaNgisi wagxambukela kulendaba wasiphoqelela.ukllba.s.ilwe.n.ayo. W ATHI ekhuluma endlini washaya imithetllO yaseNatali (Natal 
Legislative Council) uMhlonishwa uMnu Walton M.L.e. wabhekisa kanje:, ,,'.'Emva kokudabula kwebandla labadabuli (Boundary Commission) kubonakala sengathi akukho kakhulu okwenziwe phakathi kweNtilasifali nelakwaZulu. Sasihlala ngokuthu'la okukhulu futhi kungekho nolunci olwalungenza sicabange ilkuthi kungahle kubekhona impi esingayilwa nalelozwe. Emva kokudabula kodwa kwaba into esematheni ukuthi impi into eseduzane. Kwalethwa into yempi kwathiwa nokusho amasosha awahlale angabe esaya ukuyoshaywa ngumoya. Kuyo yonke lento iKoloni lalingenanto yokuba Iiyenze ngaphandle kokuthi Iikhethe amakhomishani ... Kwazeka ngo Agasti 1878 ukuthi uNdunankulu wempi uyeza, futhi namabutho afika konke futhi lokhu iKoloni Iingazange lize libuzwe noma yini." 
  UMhlonishwa uFredrick Moor (kamuva obesekuthiwa uSir Frederic Moor) wathi yena: "Konke kwasukela emgomeni owawuliphutha kuHulumeni waphesheya. Ukuba lowo Hulumeni wayengazange ayithathe iNtilasifali nakuleyo ndaba njalo iNa tali yayi'" ngazange ike ikhiphe izwi, ngabe impi ayizange ize ibe khona." 
  UMhlonishwa uMnu. Mellersh wabhekisa kanjena yen.: "Ngiphika ngihlanza okwayizolo ukuthi impi yalwela ukuvikela iNatali ukuthi yalwela ukuvikela iKoloni kuyinto ephambene kakhulu, into eyinganekwane, isithombe sengqondo." 
  UMhlonishwa uMnu. Escombe wathi: Ukuthi impi kwakuyinto eyayingase ibekhona kwaxoxwa kudala eKapa, kudala ngaphambi kokuba uNdunankulu wempi afike lapha ngo Agasti. Ngingangabazi impi into eyayivelisoshwe eKapa ngomhlaka-9 kuJuly 1878. Ngasuka lapha izinsuku zimbili KuJulayi 1878. Ngaleyonkathi ngangingaKaze ngizwe lutho ngempi yakwaZulu kodwa kuba ngumhlaka- 9 kuJulayi (eKapa) ngezwa ngezikhulu zempi ukuthi impi yamaNgisi izotheleka ngoSepthemba kuleli.

UMLOB! walencwadii uMajor Cecil Cowley wazalwa ngo 1884 endaweni etshalwa umoba nekhofi eNatali. Usaphila kahle kakhulu, isahluzeke kahle uyakwazi ukwenza izinto czahlukcne empilweni yakhe. Kwathi esesithohlongwanc esineminyaka esithupha kuphela uyisc wafa wasala wakhuliswa uSir Marshall Campbell. Wafund~ eHilton College waze waqala ukuziscbenzela cneminyaKu eyishumi nesithupha eyintatheli yeNatal Mercury. Kusukela ngo 1906 wasengena emsebcnzini wokuba ngummeIi kwelaseNatali nakwaZulu, futhi usesondelane kakhulu nabantu bakwaZulll kusukela kubafana abc!usayo kuye phezulu emakhosini ngisho nabozalo IwaseNdlunkulu. Usehlale kakhulu exoxa nabantu abadal" abasakhumbula okuningi kwesizwe sabo esikhulu okudala. Enye futhi into emsizile uMajor Cowley. maqondana nokllioba lelibhllkc ngczimpi zakwaZulu, ulwazi Iwakhe yena luqobo eminyakeni eyishumi nantathu emahuthweni am~lNgisi kanye nezinkambo zakhe phahthi naphakathi neCongo kanye neTopiya (Ethiopia) naseKenya. 
  Kuzc kube sekucishweni komthetho wokumelwa kwabantu ePhalamcnde, bekunguyena obemc!e abantu baseNatali endlini yezigele ePhalamende lase Mhlabllhlangene.
